

US STOCKS-Wall St set to open higher on earnings optimism - Reuters News

{{20170731T125629.010+0000}}US STOCKS-Wall St set to open higher on earnings optimism* Futures up: Dow 58 pts; S&P 3.25 pts; Nasdaq 13.5 pts

(Adds details, comment, updates prices)

By Sweta Singh and Ankur Banerjee

July 31 (Reuters) - U.S. stock indexes looked set to open higher on Monday as investors remained optimistic about corporate earnings in the second quarter and ahead of a clutch of economic data.

Investors have been counting on earnings to support the relatively high valuations for equities, with the S&P 500 trading at about 18 times earnings estimates for the next 12 months, above its long-term average of 15 times. [nL1N1KJ1RJ]

Of the 289 S&P 500 companies that reported results until Friday, 73 percent of them beat analyst expectations. This is above the 71 percent average over the past four quarters, according to Thomson Reuters I/B/E/S.

The S&P 500 slipped on Friday on negative reactions to earnings reports from high-profile names such as Amazon , Exxon and Starbucks and a drop in shares of tobacco companies.

"We had a choppy week last week, we had a very erratic week, so coming off a erratic week, we're getting some early morning premarket bargain hunting," said Andre Bakhos, managing director at Janlyn Capital LLC.

Apple Inc , a part of the Dow, is expected to report quarterly results after market close on Tuesday and its performance may hold the sway over tech stocks this week.

Data vying for attention includes ISM Chicago Purchasing Managers' Index data that is expected at 9:45 a.m. ET. The reading, which is an indicator of the strength of U.S. manufacturing sector, is likely to show a slight dip in July.

The Federal Reserve of Dallas will release its monthly manufacturing index for July at around 10:30 a.m. ET.

Oil prices rose on Monday, putting July was on track to become the strongest month for the commodity this year. [O/R]

"What is causing the erratic behavior is a lack of the healthcare bill, any legislation coming from the Congress," Bakhos said.

"So right now, we're going to get some hesitation, hopefully until signs come out of Washington that things will be on the move."

The seven-year Republican quest to scrap Obamacare, a major campaign vow by President Donald Trump, lay in ruins last week after the Senate failed to dismantle the healthcare law.

Dow e-minis <1YMc1> were up 58 points, or 0.27 percent, with 19,868 contracts changing hands at 8:20 a.m. ET (1220 GMT). S&P 500 e-minis were up 3.25 points, or 0.13 percent, with 132,207 contracts traded. Nasdaq 100 e-minis were up 13.5 points, or 0.23 percent, on volume of 26,173 contracts.

Scripps Network was up 1.23 percent at $87.98 premarket after Discovery Communications said it would buy the media company for $14.6 billion. [nASB0BBQK]

Charter Communications Inc up 8 percent after the U.S. cable operator said on Sunday it was not interested in buying wireless carrier Sprint Corp . [nL4N1KM1T1]

Shares of Snap Inc fell 3 percent in premarket trading as a share lockup ended, allowing for sales by early investors and pushing it further below its March initial public offering price.

(Reporting by Ankur Banerjee, Sweta Singh, Sruthi Shankar and Yashaswini Swamynathan in Bengaluru; Editing by Arun Koyyur) ((sweta.singh@thomsonreuters.com; within U.S. +1 646 223 8780, outside U.S +91 80 6749 6125; Reuters Messaging: Reuters Messaging: sweta.singh.thomsonreuters.com@reuters.net))

US STOCKS-Futures higher as investors assess earnings scorecard - 路透新闻

{{20170731T114322.391+0000}}US STOCKS-Futures higher as investors assess earnings scorecard* Futures up: Dow 50 pts; S&P 3 pts; Nasdaq 12.75 pts

By Sweta Singh

July 31 (Reuters) - U.S. stock index futures were slightly higher on Monday with investors assessing Corporate America's second quarter earnings scorecard while waiting for a clutch of economic data.

* Of the 289 S&P 500 companies that reported results until Friday, 73 percent of them beat analyst expectations. This is above the 71 percent average over the past four quarters, according to Thomson Reuters I/B/E/S.

* Investors have been counting on earnings to support the relatively high valuations for equities. The S&P 500 is trading at about 18 times earnings estimates for the next 12 months, above its long-term average of 15 times. [nL1N1KJ1RJ]

* Apple Inc , a part of the Dow, is expected to report quarterly results after market close on Tuesday and its performance may hold the sway over tech stocks this week.

* The S&P 500 slipped on Friday on negative reactions to earnings reports from high-profile names such as Amazon , Exxon and Starbucks and a drop in shares of tobacco companies.

* Data vying for attention includes ISM Chicago Purchasing Managers' Index data that is expected at 9:45 a.m. ET. The reading, which is an indicator of the strength of U.S. manufacturing sector, is likely to show a slight dip in July.

* The Federal Reserve of Dallas will release its monthly manufacturing index for July at around 10:30 a.m. ET.

* Even as oil prices were slightly down on Monday, July was on track to become the strongest month for the commodity this year. [O/R]

* Scripps Network was up 1.23 percent at $87.98 premarket after Discovery Communications said it would buy the media company for $14.6 billion. [nASB0BBQK]

* Dynavax Technologies was up 108 percent at $19.25 in heavy premarket trading after its experimental hepatitis B vaccine received positive feedback from a panel of expert advisers to the U.S. Food and Drug Administration. [nL1N1KJ1UJ]

Futures snapshot at 7:39 a.m. ET (11:39 GMT):

* S&P 500 e-minis were up 3 points, or 0.12 percent, with 123,122 contracts changing hands.

* Nasdaq 100 e-minis were up 12.75 points, or 0.22 percent, in volume of 24,251 contracts.

* Dow e-minis <1YMcv1> were up 50 points, or 0.23 percent, with 18,665 contracts changing hands.

(Reporting by Sweta Singh and Yashaswini Swamynathan in Bengaluru; Editing by Arun Koyyur) ((sweta.singh@thomsonreuters.com; within U.S. +1 646 223 8780, outside U.S +91 80 6749 6125; Reuters Messaging: Reuters Messaging: sweta.singh.thomsonreuters.com@reuters.net))

UPDATE 1-Saudi's SABIC reports 25 pct fall in Q2 net profit - Reuters News

{{20170730T103427.867+0000}}UPDATE 1-Saudi's SABIC reports 25 pct fall in Q2 net profit(Adds CEO comments on Aramco project, earnings)

July 30 (Reuters) - Saudi Basic Industries Corp <2010.SE> (SABIC) missed estimates with a 25 percent fall in second-quarter net profit on Sunday as the world's fourth-largest petrochemicals maker reported higher selling costs and lower sales.

Net profit fell to 3.71 billion riyals ($989.3 million) in the three months to June 30 from a revised 4.96 billion a year earlier, the company said in a bourse statement.

That fell well short of the 4.6 billion riyals expected by analysts.

SABIC shares fell 1.2 percent in opening trade on the kingdom's stock exchange.

Chief Executive Yousef al-Benyan said profit fall stemmed from weaker performance at its Hadeed iron and steel unit.

"The impact of our Q2 comes from Hadeed, related to inventory and slow sales," Benyan told a news conference in Riyadh.

The drop in demand for steel was seasonal, driven by the Muslim holidays of Ramadan and Eid, he said, adding the company would try to reduce expenses and increase production.

"Hopefully in the third and fourth quarters the demand will pick up, because normally these (expenses and production) are impacted by these important occasions in the second quarter," Benyan said.

SABIC, which aims to be the world's third-biggest petrochemicals producer, said prior period figures had been restated.

Like most Saudi publicly listed firms, SABIC adopted IFRS accounting standards in January.

Its plastics, fertilisers and metals are used in construction, agriculture and manufacturing.

SABIC had expected this year to be positive in terms of economic growth in key markets. The firm's earnings shot up 80 percent in the first quarter buoyed by higher prices.

Benyan told Reuters in May the firm was evaluating acquisition opportunities in the range of $3 billion to $6 billion in petrochemicals, speciality chemicals and fertilisers and aims to do the first such deal in the fourth quarter of this year. [nL8N1I442]

SABIC's expansion is driven by the need to be closer to key markets and feedstock. Constraints in new gas supplies in Saudi Arabia are forcing petrochemical producers to look abroad for expansion.

The company is making progress towards a major investment in the United States with an affiliate of Exxon Mobil .

It is also pursuing its first project with oil giant Saudi Aramco, development of an oil-to-chemicals project in Saudi Arabia which analysts see as a breakthrough in the industry.

Benyan said he expected to announce more detail on the project by the end of the third quarter. ($1 = 3.7501 riyals)

(Reporting by Katie Paul and Hadeel Al Sayegh; editing by Saeed Azhar and Jason Neely) ((Saeed.Azhar@thomsonreuters.com; +65-64035664 ; Reuters Messaging: saeed.azhar.reuters.com@reuters.net))

Saudi's SABIC Q2 net profit declines 25 pct - Reuters News

{{20170730T060056.188+0000}}Saudi's SABIC Q2 net profit declines 25 pctJuly 30 (Reuters) - Saudi Basic Industries Corp <2010.SE> (SABIC), the world's fourth-biggest petrochemicals company reported a 25 percent decline in second-quarter net profit on Sunday, amid higher selling costs and lower sales.

SABIC made a net profit of 3.71 billion riyals in the three months to June 30, down from a revised 4.96 billion riyals in the year-earlier period, the company said in a bourse statement.

SABIC said prior period figures have been restated.

SABIC, like most Saudi publicly listed firms adopted IFRS accounting standards in January this year

SABIC, which aims to be Number 3 petrochemicals producer globally, attributed the profit fall to higher cost of sales and lower sales quantities.

The company's results are closely tied to oil prices and global economic growth because its products -- plastics, fertilisers and metals -- are used extensively in construction, agriculture, industry and the manufacturing of consumer goods.

SABIC had expected this year to be positive in terms of economic growth in key markets.

CEO, Yousef al-Benyan told Reuters in May the firm is evaluating acquisition opportunities in the range of $3 billion to $6 billion in petrochemicals, speciality chemicals and fertilisers and aims to do the first such deal in the fourth quarter of this year.[nL8N1I442]

SABIC's expansion is driven by the need to be closer to key markets and feedstock.

Constraints in new gas supplies in Saudi Arabia is forcing petrochemical producers to look abroad for expansion.

The company is making progress towards major investment in the United States with an affiliate of U.S. Exxon Mobil , and its first project with oil giant Saudi Aramco for the development of oil-to-chemicals project in Saudi Arabia, which analysts see as a breakthrough in the industry.

(Reporting by Hadeel Al Sayegh; Editing by Saeed Azhar) ((Saeed.Azhar@thomsonreuters.com; +65-64035664 ; Reuters Messaging: saeed.azhar.reuters.com@reuters.net))

WRAPUP 2-Exxon Mobil profit disappoints Wall Street, Chevron shines - Reuters News

{{20170728T184730.213+0000}}WRAPUP 2-Exxon Mobil profit disappoints Wall Street, Chevron shinesBy Ernest Scheyder

HOUSTON, July 28 (Reuters) - Exxon Mobil Corp posted a rare earnings miss on Friday, the only international oil producer to do so last quarter, as production slipped in its African and Canadian operations.

Exxon's results were overshadowed by rival Chevron Corp , which easily exceeded Wall Street's expectations with a double-digit percentage increase in production.

Royal Dutch Shell Plc , Total SA and Statoil ASA this week delivered profits that topped expectations also.[nL5N1KI7KW][nL5N1KI0YM]

Chevron for years has downplayed profits to spend heavily on megaprojects in Australia, the U.S. Gulf of Mexico and elsewhere.

That spending now is boosting Chevron's profit, whereas Exxon has fewer projects about to come online and many of its older assets require more capital to maintain.

While profit rose sharply from a year earlier, the Irving, Texas-based company's production slipped about 1.0 percent.[nL1N1KJ0EC]

"Exxon continues to really struggle on getting its output up," said Edward Jones analyst Brian Youngberg.

"Chevron is going from a cash spender to a cash generator, even without commodity prices improving," he said.

Shares of Exxon fell about 2.0 percent to $79.17 in Friday afternoon trading while shares of Chevron gained more than 2.0 percent to $108.53 per share. Oil prices rose on Friday to a two-month high.[nL3N1KJ1EA]

Exxon's stock was the worst drag on the Dow Jones industrial average <.DJI>, while shares of Chevron led the index higher.

Both companies said they would continue to deploy drilling rigs and other equipment to the Permian Basin, the largest U.S. oilfield.

That expansion, along with similar plans by other U.S. shale peers, is likely to further irritate the Organization of the Petroleum Exporting Countries, which have tried with mixed success this year to tame an oversupply of crude oil.[nL5N1KF1S6][nL1N1IA0M4]

Exxon posted second-quarter net income of $3.35 billion, or 78 cents per share, compared to $1.7 billion, or 41 cents per share, a year earlier. Analysts expected earnings of 84 cents per share, according to Thomson Reuters I/B/E/S.

In Africa, where Exxon produces in Nigeria, Angola and elsewhere, production slipped 16 percent due to declining fields rates and project delays.

Imperial Oil Ltd , which is majority controlled by Exxon and operates in Canada's oil sands region, posted a net loss, denting Exxon's results from that country.[nL3N1KJ45W]

Exxon's Kearl oil sands operations in Alberta were partly offline, hurting Canadian production.

Still, Exxon sought to highlight the positive, stressing its growth opportunities in liquefied natural gas (LNG), especially in Qatar, where it has invested billions.

Despite a recent diplomatic row with its Gulf Arab neighbors, Qatar "is a very important partnership for us" and Exxon is "very interested" in expanding operations there, company executive Jeff Woodbury told investors on a Friday conference call.

Any expansion would be years away from boosting Exxon's results. Reuters reported earlier this month that Exxon Chief Executive Darren Woods has been lobbying Qatar to take part in LNG expansions.[nL8N1JW5NC]

CHEVRON SHINES

San Ramon, Calif.-based Chevron boosted output by 10 percent and cut its costs, part of what executives called a pivot to earnings growth.[nL1N1KJ0JB]

The company reported second-quarter net income of $1.45 billion, or 77 cents per share, compared to a net loss of $1.47 billion, or 78 cents per share, in the year-ago quarter.

Excluding one-time items, the company earned 91 cents per share. By that measure, analysts expected earnings of 87 cents per share, according to Thomson Reuters I/B/E/S.

Chevron's cash flow dropped more than Exxon's, when compared to the same quarter last year, but with a steady stream of projects coming online, nearly all Wall Street analysts have said they prefer Chevron more than its Texas-based rival.

Chevron's Gorgon LNG project in Australia had suffered setbacks since coming online, including several temporary shutdowns earlier this year.[nL8N1IX43X][nL8N1IH3JO][nL3N1H43V8]

But those appear to be behind the company, and Chevron said its second LNG project in Australia, at Wheatstone, should be operational later this year, further boosting profit.

(Reporting by Ernest Scheyder) ((ernest.scheyder@thomsonreuters.com; Twitter: @ErnestScheyder; +1-713-210-8512; Reuters Messaging: ernest.scheyder.thomsonreuters.com@reuters.net))

Exxon's stock was the worst drag on the Dow Jones industrial average <.DJI>, while shares of Chevron led the index higher.

Both companies said they would continue to deploy drilling rigs and other equipment to the Permian Basin, the largest U.S. oilfield.

That expansion, along with similar plans by other U.S. shale peers, is likely to further irritate the Organization of the Petroleum Exporting Countries, which have tried with mixed success this year to tame an oversupply of crude oil.[nL5N1KF1S6][nL1N1IA0M4]

Exxon posted second-quarter net income of $3.35 billion, or 78 cents per share, compared to $1.7 billion, or 41 cents per share, a year earlier. Analysts expected earnings of 84 cents per share, according to Thomson Reuters I/B/E/S.

In Africa, where Exxon produces in Nigeria, Angola and elsewhere, production slipped 16 percent due to declining fields rates and project delays.

Imperial Oil Ltd , which is majority controlled by Exxon and operates in Canada's oil sands region, posted a net loss, denting Exxon's results from that country. [nL3N1KJ45W]

Exxon's Kearl oil sands operations in Alberta were partly offline, hurting Canadian production.

Still, Exxon sought to highlight the positive, stressing its growth opportunities in liquefied natural gas (LNG), especially in Qatar, where it has invested billions.

Despite a recent diplomatic row with its Gulf Arab neighbors, Qatar "is a very important partnership for us" and Exxon is "very interested" in expanding operations there, company executive Jeff Woodbury told investors on a Friday conference call.

Any expansion would be years away from boosting Exxon's results. Reuters reported earlier this month that Exxon Chief Executive Darren Woods has been lobbying Qatar to take part in LNG expansions. [nL8N1JW5NC]

CHEVRON SHINES

San Ramon, California-based Chevron boosted output by 10 percent and cut its costs, part of what executives called a pivot to earnings growth. [nL1N1KJ0JB]

The company reported second-quarter net income of $1.45 billion, or 77 cents per share, compared to a net loss of $1.47 billion, or 78 cents per share, in the year-ago quarter.

Excluding one-time items, the company earned 91 cents per share. By that measure, analysts expected earnings of 87 cents per share, according to Thomson Reuters I/B/E/S.

Chevron's cash flow dropped more than Exxon's, when compared to the same quarter last year, but with a steady stream of projects coming online, nearly all Wall Street analysts have said they prefer Chevron more than its Texas-based rival.

Chevron's Gorgon LNG project in Australia had suffered setbacks since coming online, including several temporary shutdowns earlier this year. [nL8N1IX43X][nL8N1IH3JO][nL3N1H43V8]

But those appear to be behind the company, and Chevron said its second LNG project in Australia, at Wheatstone, should be operational later this year, further boosting profit.

BREAKINGVIEWS-Exxon looks longingly at Chevron's primed pump - Reuters Breakingviews

{{20170728T171915.290+0000}}BREAKINGVIEWS-Exxon looks longingly at Chevron's primed pump(The author is a Reuters Breakingviews columnist. The opinions expressed are her own.)

By Lauren Silva Laughlin

NEW YORK, July 28 (Reuters Breakingviews) - Exxon Mobil is stuck playing catch-up. The $336 billion oil and gas company on Friday reported vastly improved second-quarter results compared to the same period last year. But fellow integrated major Chevron outpaced it as investments it made in the Permian Basin in West Texas earlier in the cycle are starting to pay off.

These helped Chevron turn a $1.5 billion loss in the three months to June in 2016 into a $1.5 billion profit this year. Its overall production rose by 250,000 barrels a day, equivalent to a 10 percent increase over the quarter, thanks in large part to a one-third jump in Permian output.

Moreover, it has reduced operating costs in the area by 37 percent since 2015. Chief Executive John Watson has also been investing more in the region, having closed seven deals so far this year which he reckons should yield a 30 percent internal rate of return. He is also eyeing as much as 200,000 acres for purchase before the end of 2018.

Darren Woods, who took over as Exxon chief executive at the start of the year, is not in as good a position; predecessor Rex Tillerson had not committed as many resources to the Permian before he left to become U.S. secretary of state. As a consequence, Exxon's U.S. E&P division fell well short of Goldman Sachs' expectations and the company is only just breaking ground on West Texas wells on land it bought earlier this year. Production at the company fell by 1 percent to 3.9 million barrels a day.

That's part of Woods' broader plan to boost capital expenditure and put its cash pile to work that should bring relatively quick results, assuming commodity prices allow. And Exxon does, at least, have a decent investment track record: the 6.7 percent return on capital employed, according to Thomson Reuters data, that analysts expect this year is best in class.

Trouble is, rivals including Chevron are starting to cut back spending as prices fall, just as oil floods the market. Exxon may end up being a smart contrarian. If not, it'll only be able to look longingly at its competitor's primed pumps.

On Twitter https://twitter.com/TheRealLSL

CONTEXT NEWS

- Exxon Mobil, the world's largest publicly traded oil and gas company, on July 28 reported second-quarter earnings of $3.4 billion, 97 percent higher than the same period last year. Revenue rose 9 percent. At 78 cents per share the company missed the consensus estimate of sell-side analysts of 84 cents per share, according to Thomson Reuters I/B/E/S.

- Earnings in the company's upstream division were $1.2 billion, up $890 million from the second quarter last year. The company's production fell 1 percent in the quarter to 3.9 million barrels per day.

- On the same day, Chevron said it earned $1.5 billion in the second quarter, or 78 cents per share, compared with a loss of $1.5 billion in the same quarter last year. Excluding one-time items, the company's earnings per share hit 91 cents. Analysts were expecting earnings of 87 cents per share. Revenue grew 18 percent. Net oil-equivalent production was 2.8 million barrels per day, compared with 2.5 million barrels per day from a year ago.

UPDATE 2-Italy's Eni confident of dividend even with lower oil prices - Reuters News

{{20170728T160312.848+0000}}UPDATE 2-Italy's Eni confident of dividend even with lower oil prices* Adjusted net profit 463 mln euros vs 317 mln loss year ago

* Cash flow up 56 pct to 2.7 billion euros

* First half oil and gas output up 6.1 pct

* 2017 interim dividend of 0.4 euros

(Recasts lead, adds CEO comments, analyst)

By Stephen Jewkes

MILAN, July 28 (Reuters) - Italian oil major Eni said on Friday its dividend was safe even at lower oil prices thanks to a string of major discoveries underpinning output growth and cash generation for the years to come.

Eni , the most active of the foreign oil majors in Africa, has one of the best discovery records in the industry, with large gas fields in Mozambique and Egypt. More recently it also made an oil find in Mexico.

Under its so-called "dual exploration" strategy, the company aims to sell down stakes in fields it operates to raise cash to fund future development and support dividends.

"We have all the tools to cope with oil at $45 a barrel," CEO Claudio Descalzi told analysts on a second-quarter results call when asked about dividend sustainability.

"We are able to tackle this situation, and we won't be using scrip dividends," he said, referring to a practice where investors are offered shares in place of cash.

Eni, whose cash flow jumped 56 pct to 2.7 billion euros in the second quarter, has committed to paying a dividend in 2017 of 0.80 euros per share.

Investors in oil firms have been unnerved by weak oil prices, which have struggled to hold gains that followed a deal between the Organization of the Petroleum Exporting Countries and some other producers to cut crude production from January.

Prices climbed above $58 a barrel in January, recovering from the 2016 lows of just $27. But Brent has since slipped back and is now hovering around $52, leading banks to downgrade price forecasts and investor concerns about shareholder returns.

Eni, which has pledged to cut spending this year by about 18 percent, earmarked about 32 billion euros of investments in its four-year business plan in March.

Descalzi said there was room to reduce those investments if needed. "In the second half of the plan 50 percent of the capex is not yet committed ... we have flexibility," he said.

OUTPUT AHEAD

Eni, which will benefit from a ramp-up at Kazakhstan's giant Kashagan field, said it expected output this year to jump 5 percent to 1.84 million barrels per day as projects in Angola, Ghana, Indonesia and Egypt come on stream ahead of schedule.

Longer term, it expects output to rise 3 percent a year.

Eni said its discovery in the Gulf of Mexico could contain more than the 1.3 billion barrels of oil equivalent in place estimated so far. It said it would decide early next year whether to proceed with investment there.

"We own 100 percent of Mexico and it's clearly one of our future targets (for selling down)," Descalzi said.

Eni, which has agreed to sell stakes in its Mozambique and Egyptian fields to ExxonMobil and Rosneft , expects to raise 4 billion euros this year from disposals.

Santander oil analyst Jason Kenney, who was upbeat about Eni on a three- to five-year outlook, said the market had underestimated the value of Eni's dual exploration strategy.

"Investors have proved unwilling to support Eni for its valuable discovered resource potential," he said.

Shares in Eni closed up 0.3 percent, broadly in line with the European oil and gas sector <.SXEP>. Milan's blue-chip index <.FTMIB> closed down 0.9 percent.

(Additional reporting by Valentina Za; Editing by Edmund Blair) ((stephen.jewkes@thomsonreuters.com; +39.0266129695; Reuters Messaging: stephen.jewkes.thomsonreuters.com@reuters.net))

BUZZ-Exxon, Chevron go separate ways after their qtrly results - Reuters News

{{20170728T155246.823+0000}}BUZZ-Exxon, Chevron go separate ways after their qtrly results** Oil major shares see different reactions to their qtrly results released Fri: Chevron gaining, while Exxon Mobil comes under pressure

** Chevron up ~2 pct after co beat the adj EPS estimate by nearly 5 pct, while Exxon down ~2 pct after it came in shy of adj EPS estimate by about 7 pct [nL1N1KJ0JB] [nL1N1KJ0EC]

** With Chevron, "compared to our estimate, half of the upstream earnings beat is driven by the lower than expected exploration expenses and the rest is due to better production volumes," analysts at Barclays wrote

** Adding that the market may view the co's strong ops cash flow favorably

** Barclays recently reiterated a positive outlook on energy majors, saying sentiment has "rarely sunk to such depressed levels over the last 25 years."

** Overall analyst opinion is skewed more positively toward CVX which has a composite buy rating vs hold for XOM (Thomson Reuters data)

** Additionally, in terms of upside vs median PTs, CVX currently offers gain potential of 10.5 pct vs just 4.6 pct for XOM

** While U.S. oil prices are down in 2017, they have rallied sharply in recent sessions, largely in the wake of a decline in U.S. inventories and OPEC's efforts to curb production

** Exxon down 12.6 pct YTD, while Chevron has lost 8.5 pct [nL1N1JH1R8]

** XOM and CVX nearly 40 pct weight in Energy Select Sector SPDR Fund , which is flat in Fri trade [nL1N1KH0J3]

Lucro da petroleira Exxon quase dobra, mas fica abaixo de expectativas - Reuters (Portuguese, Brazil)

{{20170728T143654.135+0000}}Lucro da petroleira Exxon quase dobra, mas fica abaixo de expectativas28 Jul (Reuters) - A Exxon Mobil , maior petroleira com ações negociadas em bolsa do mundo, disse nesta sexta-feira que seu lucro trimestral quase dobrou devido a maiores margens em suas operações fora dos Estados Unidos, mas ainda assim os resultados ficaram abaixo das expectativas do mercado.

As ações da companhia, com sede em Irving, no Texas, caíram cerca de 1,9 por cento após a divulgação do resultado, em negociações antes da abertura do mercado.

Enquanto o portfólio da Exxon nos EUA, incluindo seus projetos de xisto, registrou perdas, as operações de gás e petróleo ao redor do mundo tiveram uma alta de 89 por cento na lucratividade.

A companhia vendeu mais gasolina e querosene no trimestre, impulsionando os ganhos, mas as vendas de químicos caíram em parte devido a custos com manutenção de unidades e margens fracas.

"Nosso trabalho é aumentar o valor no longo-prazo investindo em nosso portfólio integrado de oportunidades que podem ter sucesso independente das condições de mercado", disse o presidente da companhia, Darren Woods, em nota.

A companhia teve lucro líquido de 3,35 bilhões de dólares no segundo trimestre, ou 78 centavos de dólar por ação, ante 1,7 bilhão, ou 41 centavos por ação no mesmo período do ano passado. Analistas esperavam lucros de 84 centavos por ação, segundo pesquisa da Thomson Reuters.

A produção da companhia caiu 1 por cento, para 3,9 milhões de barris de óleo equivalente por dia.

(Por Ernest Scheyder)

POINT MARCHÉS-Wall Street ouvre en baisse, Amazon pèse - Reuters (French)

{{20170728T140709.533+0000}}POINT MARCHÉS-Wall Street ouvre en baisse, Amazon pèsePARIS, 28 juillet (Reuters) - Les indices de Wall Street ouvrent en recul vendredi pour une nouvelle séance dominée par les résultats, en particulier ceux d'Amazon dont la forte baisse du bénéfice impacte la tendance.

Vers 14h05 GMT, l'indice Dow Jones <.DJI> cède 26,43 points, soit 0,12%, à 21.770,12. Le Standard & Poor's 500 <.SPX>, plus large, perd 0,28% à 2.468,37 et le Nasdaq Composite <.IXIC> recule de 0,39% à 6.357,53.

Les résultats trimestriels sont surveillés de près par les investisseurs pour savoir si la forte valorisation actuelle du marché est justifiée dans un contexte de faible inflation.

D'après Thomson Reuters I/B/E/S, les bénéfices sont attendus en hausse de 10,7% au deuxième trimestre contre 8% prévus au début du mois.

Les craintes sur les capacités de Donald Trump à légiférer pour relancer la croissance reviennent sur le devant de la scène après le rejet par le Sénat américain d'un texte prévoyant une abrogation partielle de la loi sur l'assurance-maladie dite "Obamacare".

Une décision qui pourrait mettre fin aux efforts déployés depuis sept ans par le Parti républicain pour supprimer cette réforme emblématique de la présidence de Barack Obama, l'une des principales promesses de campagne de Donald Trump. [nL5N1KJ1HY]

"Il semble que l'Obamacare soit devenu un cauchemar pour Trump et pas une bonne nouvelle pour les marchés non plus", estime Naeem Aslam, analyste marchés chez ThinkMarkets.

Sur le plan des statistiques, la croissance de l'économie américaine a accéléré au deuxième trimestre avec la hausse de la consommation des ménages et de l'investissement des entreprises, ce qui confirme que le trou d'air des trois premiers mois de l'année était bien passager. [nL5N1KJ550]

A cette annonce, le dollar a momentanément creusé ses pertes avant de revenir quasiment à son niveau initial (-0,3%) face un panier de devises de référence <.DXY>. L'euro en profite et gagne 0,4%.

L'indice sectoriel des biens de consommation non essentiels <.SPLRCD>, dans lequel cote Amazon , signe de loin la plus mauvaise performance de la séance (-7,24%).

L'indice technologique cède lui 0,15% <.SPLRCT>.

Le géant du commerce électronique laisse 3,65% après avoir annoncé jeudi un bénéfice du deuxième trimestre en baisse de 77%, sans exclure une perte opérationnelle au troisième. [nL5N1KIBVE]

Exxon , première capitalisation pétrolière mondiale, perd 2,87%, plus forte baisse du Dow, après fait état vendredi d'un quasi-doublement de son bénéfice trimestriel grâce à la nette amélioration des marges de ses activités en dehors des Etats-Unis. [nL5N1KJ50K]

A l'opposé, Intel gagne 1,40% grâce à une hausse plus marquée que prévu de son chiffre d'affaires du deuxième trimestre [nL5N1KIBI9].

Il est suivi de Chevron qui a renoué avec le bénéfice au deuxième trimestre grâce à une baisse des coûts et à une nette hausse de la production. [nL5N1KJ5B1]

L'action prend 1,96%.

Le moteur de recherches chinois Baidu a annoncé des résultats trimestriels meilleurs que prévu; l'action progresse de 6,92%.

Plus forte baisse du S&P 500, Goodyear Tire & Rubber chute de 9,92%, lésé par une baisse plus forte que prévu de ses ventes trimestrielles.

Autre baisse notable, Starbucks dégringole de 7,18%, le groupe américain de cafés s'étant montré prudent pour le trimestre en cours. [nL5N1KIBUD]

Mattel abandonne 8,57% à la suite de résultats trimestriels en-deçà des attentes.

En Europe, les indices actions perdent entre 0,4% et 1,3%.

* Pour les valeurs à suivre, cliquez sur [nL5N1KIC0L]

ACTUALIZA 1-Exxon Mobil casi duplica su ganancia trimestral, pero incumple expectativas de Wall Street  - Reuters (Spanish)

{{20170728T140707.796+0000}}ACTUALIZA 1-Exxon Mobil casi duplica su ganancia trimestral, pero incumple expectativas de Wall Street (Amplía información)

28 jul (Reuters) - Exxon Mobil Corp, el mayor productor de petróleo del mundo que cotiza en bolsa, dijo el viernes que sus ganancias trimestrales casi se duplicaron por los crecientes márgenes de sus operaciones fuera de Estados Unidos, pero los resultados incumplieron las expectativas de Wall Street.

Las acciones de la empresa con sede Irving, Texas, caían cerca de 2,8 por ciento en las primeras operaciones de Wall Street.

Si bien la cartera de Exxon en Estados Unidos, que incluye sus proyectos de esquisto, perdió dinero, las operaciones globales de gas y petróleo de la empresa registraron un aumento del 69 por ciento en sus ganancias.

La compañía vendió más gasolina y queroseno en el trimestre, pero las ventas de productos químicos cayeron debido en parte a costos de mantenimiento y unos márgenes débiles.

"Nuestro trabajo es aumentar valor a largo plazo con la inversión en nuestra cartera integral de oportunidades, que prospera independiente de las condiciones del mercado", dijo el presidente ejecutivo de la petrolera, Darren Woods, en un comunicado.

La compañía registró una utilidad neta de 3.350 millones de dólares, o 78 centavos por acción, en comparación con los 1.700 millones de dólares, o 41 centavos por acción, del mismo periodo de un año antes. Los analistas esperaban ganancias de 84 centavos por acción, según Thomson Reuters I/B/E/S.

La producción cayó un 1 por ciento a 3,9 millones de barriles de petróleo equivalente por día.

Los resultados se conocen en momentos en que Exxon lucha con sus accionistas y otros sectores por los problemas vinculados al cambio climático.

Exxon se ha visto envuelto en una fuerte disputa a raíz de unos documentos relacionados al cambio climático con el fiscal general del estado de Nueva York, Eric Schneiderman, quien busca sancionar al productor de petróleo por lo que asegura son revelaciones públicas engañosas.

Los accionistas de Exxon aprobaron en mayo una resolución en que piden a la compañía emitir un informe sobre cómo el cambio climático afecta las operaciones. La votación, que no era vinculante, se aprobó con el 62 por ciento de los votos emitidos y fue una inusual derrota para la gerencia de Exxon.

(Reporte de Ernest Scheyder. Editado en español por Rodrigo Charme) ((ernest.scheyder@thomsonreuters.com; Mesa de Edición en español +562 2437 44 00. Twitter: @ReutersLatam)) ((REUTERS GB))Copyright (c) 2017 Thomson Reuters

Exxon und Chevron machen dank Ölpreisanstieg Milliarden - Reuters (German)

{{20170728T132850.792+0000}}Exxon und Chevron machen dank Ölpreisanstieg MilliardenHouston, 28. Jul (Reuters) - Der deutlich erholte Ölpreis spült den großen US-Energiekonzernen wieder Milliarden in die Kassen. Der größte börsennotierte Multi Exxon verdoppelte im abgelaufenen Quartal seinen Gewinn nahezu, der Rivale Chevron schrieb nach einem Verlust im vergangenen Jahr wieder schwarze Zahlen. Auch die europäischen Konkurrenten fuhren wieder satte Gewinne ein.[nL5N1KI24Z] Derzeit liegt der Ölpreis bei rund 50 Dollar und damit um einiges höher als noch im Frühjahr 2016, als ein Barrel (159 Liter) lediglich 37 Dollar kostete. Hintergrund ist die vereinbarte Förderbremse der Organisation Erdöl exportierender Länder (Opec), die erst kürzlich bis März 2018 verlängert wurde.

Während des Ölpreisverfalls hatten die Ölmultis teils drastische Sparprogramme aufgelegt. Davon profitiert Chevron. Der Gewinn betrug 1,45 Milliarden Dollar nach einen Verlust von 1,47 Milliarden Dollar im Vorjahr. Konkurrent Exxon machte einen Gewinn von 3,35 Milliarden Dollar nach 1,7 Milliarden Dollar. Vor allem der Gewinn der weltweiten Öl- und Gasproduktion schoss in die Höhe. In den USA, wo auch aus Schiefer Öl und Gas gewonnen wird, schrieb Exxon jedoch rote Zahlen. Exxon-Aktien gaben im vorbörslichen Handel nach, Analysten hatten dem Konzern mehr zugetraut.

LEAD 1-Exxon Mobil-Bénéfice doublé mais inférieur au consensus - Reuters (French)

{{20170728T131204.595+0000}}LEAD 1-Exxon Mobil-Bénéfice doublé mais inférieur au consensus(Actualisé avec des précisions, cours de Bourse)

28 juillet (Reuters) - Exxon Mobil , première capitalisation pétrolière mondiale, a fait état vendredi d'un quasi-doublement de son bénéfice trimestriel grâce à la nette amélioration des marges de ses activités en dehors des Etats-Unis.

Pourtant, le bénéfice est inférieur au consensus, ce qui explique que l'action du groupe d'Irving (Texas) perdait 1,9% en avant-Bourse.

Si l'activité d'Exxon aux Etats-Unis, schistes compris, a perdu de l'argent, les opérations gazières et pétrolières internationales ont vu leur bénéfice bondir de 69%.

Le pétrolier a vendu plus d'essence et de kérosène durant le trimestre mais les ventes du segment chimie ont fléchi, en raison notamment de coûts de maintenance.

Le bénéfice est ressorti à 3,35 milliards de dollars (2,86 milliards d'euros) au deuxième trimestre, soit 78 cents par action, contre 1,7 milliard de dollars (41 cents) un an auparavant. Le consensus Thomson Reuters I/B/E/S donnait un bénéfice par action de 84 cents.

La production a baissé de 1% à 3,9 millions de barils équivalent pétrole par jour.

Exxon doit faire face à une offensive du procureur général de New York Eric Schneidermann qui estime que le pétrolier a trompé le public concernant la question des changements climatiques.

Les actionnaires d'Exxon ont adopté en mai une résolution qui impose à Exxon de soumettre un rapport sur les conséquences pour ses opérations des changements climatiques. Le vote, non contraignant, a constitué l'un des rares reverse qu'ait subi la direction.

(Ernest Scheyder, Marc Joanny pour le service français, édité par Wilfrid Exbrayat) ((Service économique. Tel 01 49 49 54 15 ;))Copyright (c) 2017 Thomson Reuters

USA-Les valeurs à suivre à Wall Street (actualisé) - Reuters (French)

{{20170728T130709.735+0000}}USA-Les valeurs à suivre à Wall Street (actualisé)(Actualisé avec Exxon Mobil, Chevron, Merck, Goodyear, Baker Hughes, American Airlines, Rockwell Collins, cours avant-Bourse)

NEW YORK, 28 juillet (Reuters) - Principales valeurs à suivre vendredi à Wall Street où les contrats à terme signalent une ouverture en baisse de l'ordre de 0,2% pour le Dow Jones <.DJI>, de 0,2% pour le S&P-500 <.SPX> et de 0,5% pour le Nasdaq <.IXIC> :

* AMAZON.COM a publié jeudi un bénéfice du deuxième trimestre en baisse de 77% et n'a pas exclu une perte opérationnelle au troisième en raison d'importants investissements consentis par le géant du commerce électronique dans des segments tels que les contenus vidéo et dans des pays, tels l'Inde, connaissant une croissance rapide. Le titre perd 2,7% à 1.017,49 dollars en avant-Bourse. [nL5N1KIBVE]

* EXXON MOBIL , première capitalisation pétrolière mondiale, a fait état vendredi d'un quasi-doublement de son bénéfice trimestriel grâce à la nette amélioration des marges de ses activités en dehors des Etats-Unis. [nL5N1KJ5CK]

* CHEVRON a renoué avec le bénéfice au deuxième trimestre grâce à une baisse des coûts et à une nette hausse de la production. [nL5N1KJ5B1]

* MERCK & CO a fait état vendredi d'un bond de 61,5% de son bénéfice trimestriel, lequel dépasse largement le consensus, grâce à la forte demande pour le Keytruda, son principal médicament d'immuno-oncologie. Le titre prend 1,2% en avant-Bourse. [nL5N1KJ4WY]

* INTEL a publié jeudi une hausse plus marquée que prévu de son chiffre d'affaires du deuxième trimestre, le géant américain des semi-conducteurs ayant vu ses performances commerciales dopées par ses activités centres de données et PC. Le groupe a également annoncé une nouvelle révision à la hausse de ses perspectives annuelles. Le titre gagne 0,8% dans des échanges d'avant-Bourse. [nL5N1KIBI9]

* STARBUCKS a publié jeudi des résultats trimestriels conformes aux attentes des analystes mais le groupe américain de cafés s'est montré prudent pour le trimestre en cours au vu d'une faiblesse de ses performances aux Etats-Unis tout en annonçant la fermeture de la totalité de ses 379 boutiques Teavana. Le titre Starbucks perd 6,2% en avant-Bourse. [nL5N1KIBUD]

* ROCKWELL COLLINS - L'équipementier de l'aéronautique américain a annoncé une hausse de 57% de son chiffre d'affaires trimestriel grâce à l'acquisition de B/E Aerospace, mais une baisse de son bénéfice en raison des coûts associés à cette transaction.

* ABBVIE a fait état vendredi d'une hausse de 18,9% de son bénéfice trimestriel grâce à une demande en hausse pour son médicament vedette, Humira.

* BAKER HUGHUES , racheté par General Electric pour créer le numéro deux du secteur parapétrolier, a annoncé un perte trimestrielle moins importante qu'il y a un an à la même période.

* ELECTRONIC ARTS a fait état jeudi d'un chiffre d'affaires du premier trimestre 2017-2018 supérieur aux attentes grâce aux ventes soutenues de titres tels que "Battlefield 1" et "The Sims" mais l'éditeur de jeux vidéo a en revanche déçu les investisseurs avec ses prévisions pour le trimestre en cours. En avant-Bourse, le titre EA recule de 2,6%.

* AMERICAN AIRLINES cède 2% en avant-Bourse malgré une hausse de son bénéfice ajusté et de son chiffre d'affaires trimestriels.

* BAIDU a annoncé des résultats trimestriels meilleurs que prévu, le moteur de recherche sur internet chinois coté aux Etats-Unis s'étant remis de l'enquête dont il a fait l'objet en Chine après la mort d'un étudiant ayant utilisé le moteur de recherche du groupe pour trouver un traitement de son cancer. En avant-Bourse, l'action progresse de 4%.

* MATTEL a publié des résultats trimestriels en-deçà des attentes, les ventes soutenues de jouets dérivés du film "Cars 3" n'ayant pas réussi à compenser les piètres performances commerciales des marques phares du groupes telles que Barbie et Fisher-Price aux Etats-Unis. En après-Bourse, le titre cédait près de 5,6%.

* EXPEDIA a fait état d'un chiffre d'affaires trimestriel légèrement supérieur aux attentes et le groupe d'agences de voyage en ligne a également confirmé ses prévisions annuelles. L'action gagne 1,5% en avant-Bourse.

* GOODYEAR TIRE & RUBBER a publié une baisse plus forte que prévu de ses ventes trimestrielles, lésé par une moindre demande pour les pneumatiques. Le premier pneumaticien américain a abaissé ses prévisions pour son résultat d'exploitation. Le titre chute de 8,7% en avant-Bourse.

EARNINGS-TICKER-Chevron macht wieder Gewinn - Reuters (German)

{{20170728T124053.734+0000}}EARNINGS-TICKER-Chevron macht wieder Gewinn28. Jul (Reuters) - Zahlreiche Firmen veröffentlichen dieser Tage ihre aktuelle Quartalsbilanz. Es folgt in Kurzform ein Überblick über einige Ergebnisse vom Freitag:

14.32 Uhr - Chevron hat im abgelaufenen Quartal wieder Gewinn gemacht. Hintergrund waren gesunkene Kosten und eine gestiegene Produktion. Der Nettogewinn des Ölkonzerns belief sich auf 1,45 Milliarden Dollar. Ein Jahr zuvor stand noch ein Verlust von 1,47 Milliarden Dollar in der Bilanz.

14.05 Uhr - Der Ölkonzern Exxon Mobil hat seinen Gewinn im abgelaufenen Quartal fast verdoppelt. Der Überschuss legte auf 3,35 Milliarden Dollar zu nach 1,7 Milliarden ein Jahr zuvor. Exxon förderte allerdings weniger Öl, die Produktion fiel ein Prozent.

13.38 Uhr - Steigende Ticketpreise und ein höheres Passagieraufkommen verhelfen American Airlines zu mehr Umsatz. Die Erlöse legten im abgelaufenen Quartal um 7,2 Prozent auf 11,11 Milliarden Dollar zu. Dennoch fiel der Nettogewinn auf 803 Millionen Dollar von zuvor 950 Millionen Dollar.

13.32 Uhr - Goodyear hat Mühe beim Verkauf seiner Reifen. Der Überschuss fiel im abgelaufenen Quartal um 27,2 Prozent auf 147 Millionen Dollar. Mit 3,69 Milliarden Dollar setzte der Konzern knapp fünf Prozent weniger um als vor einem Jahr.

12.51 Uhr - Der US-Pharmakonzern Merck & Co punktet mit seinem neuartigen Krebsmittel Keytruda. Dank der guten Verkäufe des Medikaments schoss der Nettogewinn im abgelaufenen Quartal um 61,5 Prozent auf 1,95 Milliarden Dollar nach oben. Der Umsatz stieg binnen Jahresfrist auf 9,93 von 9,84 Milliarden Dollar.

12.07 Uhr - Der Flugzeug- und Zugbauer Bombardier hat im abgelaufenen Quartal mit 4,1 Milliarden Dollar fünf Prozent weniger eingenommen als ein Jahr zuvor. Dennoch erzielte der kanadische Konzern einen bereinigten Nettogewinn von 39 Millionen Dollar. Im Vorjahreszeitraum war noch ein Verlust von 83 Millionen Dollar angefallen.

09.25 Uhr - Der Waschanlagenbauer Washtec hat im ersten Halbjahr den Umsatz um fast ein Viertel auf knapp 210 Millionen Euro gesteigert, während der Gewinn vor Steuern um mehr als 60 Prozent auf 25 Millionen Euro sprang. Im Gesamtjahr will das Unternehmen nun mindestens einen Umsatz von 420 Millionen Euro und eine Gewinnmarge von zwölf Prozent schaffen.

09.10 Uhr - Der Triebwerksbauer MTU Aero hat im zweiten Quartal bei Umsatz und Ergebnis die Erwartungen des Finanzmarktes übertroffen. Das Unternehmen erwirtschaftete einen operativen Gewinn von 164 (Prognose: 148) Millionen Euro und einen Umsatz von 1,286 (1,27) Milliarden Euro. Für das Gesamtjahr peilt es nun Erlöse von 5,3 statt 5,1 bis 5,2 Milliarden Euro an.

09.00 Uhr - Der französische Autokonzern Renault hat im ersten Halbjahr bei Absatz und Gewinn neue Rekorde eingefahren. Der operative Gewinn stieg um fast ein Fünftel auf 1,82 Milliarden Euro. Netto standen 2,4 Milliarden Euro zu Buche - nicht zuletzt dank eines hohen Gewinnbeitrags der Beteiligung Nissan<7201.T>, deren Ergebnis sich um mehr als 70 Prozent verbesserte.

08.27 Uhr - Der britische Telekomkonzern BT hat im abgelaufenen Quartal einen 42-prozentigen Einbruch des Vorsteuergewinns auf 418 Millionen Pfund (rund 468 Millionen Euro) hinnehmen müssen. Sonderlasten nach einem Bilanzskandal in Italien und einer Einigung mit der Deutschen Telekom und der französischen Orange waren dafür verantwortlich.

08.20 Uhr - Der Verkauf von Geschäftsteilen in Afrika kommt die britische Großbank Barclays teuer zu stehen. Durch die Trennung entstand in der Bilanz des ersten Halbjahres ein Verlust von 1,2 Milliarden Pfund, wie das Institut am Freitag mitteilte. Ohne diesen Sondereffekt lag der Halbjahresgewinn vor Steuern bei 2,3 Milliarden Pfund und damit 300 Millionen Pfund höher als im ersten Halbjahr 2016. Analysten hatten von den Briten allerdings einen Vorsteuergewinn von 2,7 Milliarden Pfund erwartet.

08.10 Uhr - Der französische Versorger Engie hat seinen Umsatz in der ersten Jahreshälfte leicht auf 33,1 Milliarden Euro gesteigert. Der Gewinn stagnierte bei fünf Milliarden Euro. Der Konzern bestätigte seine Jahresziele und sieht sich beim Umbau, der im kommenden Jahr abgeschlossen werden soll, über Plan.

08.00 Uhr - Die in Paris ansässige Mehrländer-Börse Euronext hat trotz der mauen Aktivität vieler Anleger im zweiten Quartal ihren Gewinn gesteigert. Das operative Ergebnis sei auf 79,2 (206: 77,7) Millionen Euro gestiegen, teilte der Betreiber von Kassa- und Derivate-Börsen in Paris, Amsterdam, Brüssel, London und Lissabon mit. Während andere Börsenbetreiber wie die Deutsche Börse teilweise von schwächeren Umsätzen berichtet hatten, stieg der tägliche Derivatehandel auf Euronext-Plattformen im zweiten Quartal um 27,3 Prozent.

07.50 Uhr - Die Fluggesellschaft Air France-KLM hat im zweiten Quartal von einem anziehenden Reisegeschäft profitiert und ihren Umsatz um 1,5 Prozent steigern können. Der operative Gewinn lag mit 496 Millionen Euro leicht über den Erwartungen von Branchenanalysten. Der französisch-niederländische Konzern veröffentlichte keine Jahresprognose, Analysten erwarten jedoch einen Jahresgewinn von rund 1,3 Milliarden Euro.

07.45 Uhr - Der französische Energieriese Electricite de France hat im ersten Halbjahr einen deutlichen Gewinnrückgang verkraften müssen. Das operative Ergebnis sei um ein Fünftel auf sieben Milliarden Euro abgerutscht, teilte das Unternehmen mit und machte dafür "unvorteilhafte Marktbedingungen" verantwortlich. Unter dem Strich blieb ein Gewinn von zwei Milliarden Euro - ein Minus von 3,7 Prozent. Seine Jahresziele bestätigte der Konzern.

07.40 Uhr - Der IT-Vermieter Grenke hat seinen Gewinn im ersten Halbjahr um fast 20 Prozent auf 78,8 Millionen Euro gesteigert und erhöht deshalb seine Prognose für das Gesamtjahr leicht. Es werde nun ein Jahresgewinn zwischen 118 und 124 Millionen Euro erwartet. Bislang war das Unternehmen von 113 bis 123 Millionen Euro ausgegangen.

07.32 Uhr - Der französische Gasekonzern Air Liquide hat im ersten Halbjahr Umsatz und Gewinn kräftig gesteigert. Unter dem Strich erwirtschaftete der Konkurrent des deutschen Linde-Konzerns in den ersten sechs Monaten 928 Millionen Euro, ein Plus von 14,5 Prozent. Der operstive Gewinn sprang sogar um mehr als 20 Prozent nach oben.

07.25 Uhr - Die spanische Großbank Santander hat dank eines brummenden Geschäfts in ihrem größten Markt Brasilien den Gewinn im zweiten Quartal um fast 40 Prozent auf 1,75 Milliarden Euro gesteigert. Das Institut hatte Anfang Juni den angeschlagenen heimischen Konkurrenten Banco Popular übernommen.

07.20 Uhr - Der erwartete Gewinnrückgang bei der französischen Großbank BNP Paribas fiel im zweiten Quartal dank Kostensenkungen und eines überraschend guten Geschäfts im Investmentbanking niedriger aus als erwartet. Der Nettogewinn von Frankreichs größtem börsennotierten Kreditinstitut sank zwischen April und Ende Juni um 6,4 Prozent auf knapp 2,4 Milliarden Euro. Von Reuters befragte Analysten hatten mit einem Gewinnrückgang auf 1,9 Milliarden Euro gerechnet.

07.10 Uhr - Der Spezialsoftwareanbieter Nemetschek hat im ersten Halbjahr seinen Umsatz um ein Fünftel auf 194 Millionen Euro gesteigert. Der operative Gewinn erreichte 51,7 Millionen Euro, was einer Rendite von 26,6 Prozent entspricht. Das Unternehmen beließ seinen Ausblick für das Gesamtjahr 2017 unverändert.

(Zusammengestellt in den Redaktionen Berlin und Frankfurt. Bei Rückfragen wenden Sie sich bitte an die Redaktionsleitung unter den Telefonnummern +49 69 7565 1232 oder +49 30 2888 5168.)Copyright (c) 2017 Thomson Reuters

UPDATE 1-Exxon profit nearly doubles, but falls short of expectations - Reuters News

{{20170728T122937.641+0000}}UPDATE 1-Exxon profit nearly doubles, but falls short of expectations(Adds earnings comparison, stock, details)

By Ernest Scheyder

July 28 (Reuters) - Exxon Mobil Corp , the world's largest publicly traded oil producer, said on Friday its quarterly profit nearly doubled on surging margins at its operations outside the United States, but results fell shy of Wall Street's expectations.

Shares of Irving, Texas-based Exxon fell about 1.9 percent in premarket trading to $79.30.

While Exxon's U.S. portfolio, including its shale projects, lost money, Exxon's gas and oil operations across the world posted a 69 percent jump in profit.

The company sold more gasoline and kerosene in the quarter, boosting the bottom line as well, but sales of chemicals slipped due in part to plant maintenance costs and weak margins.

"Our job is to grow long-term value by investing in our integrated portfolio of opportunities that succeed regardless of market conditions," Chief Executive Darren Woods said in a statement.

The company posted second-quarter net income of $3.35 billion, or 78 cents per share, compared to $1.7 billion, or 41 cents per share, a year earlier. Analysts expected earnings of 84 cents per share, according to Thomson Reuters I/B/E/S.

Production fell about 1.0 percent to 3.9 million barrels of oil equivalent per day.

The results come as Exxon battles its shareholders and others over climate change issues.

Exxon has been locked in an aggressive back-and-forth skirmish over climate change documents with New York State Attorney General Eric Schneiderman, who has sought to punish the oil producer for what he says are misleading public disclosures.[nL1N1IZ0N6]

Exxon's shareholders in May approved a resolution in May that called for the company to issue a report on how climate change affects operations. The vote, which was non-binding, passed with 62 percent of ballots cast and was a rare defeat for Exxon's management.[nL1N1IX15V]

(Reporting by Ernest Scheyder; Editing by Bernadette Baum) ((ernest.scheyder@thomsonreuters.com; Twitter: @ErnestScheyder; +1-713-210-8512; Reuters Messaging: ernest.scheyder.thomsonreuters.com@reuters.net))

Exxon Mobil quasi raddoppia utili nel trimestre - Reuters (Italian)

{{20170728T122448.984+0000}}Exxon Mobil quasi raddoppia utili nel trimestre28 luglio (Reuters) - Exxon Mobil , la più grande compagnia petrolifera quotata in Borsa, ha quasi raddoppiato i suoi utili trimestrali grazie all'incremento dei margini delle attività fuori dagli Usa.

L'utile netto del secondo trimestre è salito a 3,35 miliardi di dollari, pari a 78 cent per azione, contro 1,7 miliardi (41 cent per azione) di un anno prima.

La produzione è scesa di circa 1% a 3,9 milioni di barili di olio equivalente al giorno.

Exxon Mobil casi duplica su ganancia trimestral - Reuters (Spanish)

{{20170728T122129.221+0000}}Exxon Mobil casi duplica su ganancia trimestral28 jul (Reuters) - Exxon Mobil Corp , el mayor productor de petróleo del mundo que cotiza en bolsa, dijo el viernes que sus ganancias trimestrales casi se duplicaron por los crecientes márgenes de sus operaciones fuera de Estados Unidos.

La compañía registró una utilidad neta de 3.350 millones de dólares, o 78 centavos por acción, en comparación con los 1.700 millones de dólares, o 41 centavos por acción, del mismo periodo de un año antes.

La producción cayó un 1 por ciento a 3,9 millones de barriles de petróleo equivalente por día.

Exxon Mobil-Doublement des profits au T2  - Reuters (French)

{{20170728T121555.216+0000}}Exxon Mobil-Doublement des profits au T2 28 juillet (Reuters) - Exxon Mobil , première capitalisation pétrolière mondiale, a fait état vendredi d'un quasi-doublement de son bénéfice trimestriel grâce à la nette amélioration des marges de ses activités en dehors des Etats-Unis.

Le bénéfice est ressorti à 3,35 milliards de dollars (2,86 milliards d'euros) au deuxième trimestre, soit 78 cents par action, contre 1,7 milliard de dollars (41 cents) un an auparavant.

La production a baissé de 1% à 3,9 millions de barils équivalent pétrole par jour.

L'action perdait 1,2% à 79,15 dollars en avant-Bourse.

Exxon Mobil quarterly profit nearly doubles  - Reuters News

{{20170728T120603.706+0000}}Exxon Mobil quarterly profit nearly doubles July 28 (Reuters) - Exxon Mobil Corp , the world's largest publicly traded oil producer, said on Friday its quarterly profit nearly doubled on surging margins at its operations outside the United States.

The company posted net income of $3.35 billion, or 78 cents per share, compared to $1.7 billion, or 41 cents per share, a year earlier.

Production fell about 1 percent to 3.9 million barrels of oil equivalent per day.

What to Watch in the Day Ahead - Friday, July 28 - 路透新闻

{{20170727T184128.593+0000}}What to Watch in the Day Ahead - Friday, July 28(The Day Ahead is an email and PDF publication that includes the day's major stories and events, analyses and other features. To receive The Day Ahead, Eikon users can register at [DAY/US]. Thomson One users can register at RT/DAY/US. All times in ET/GMT)

The U.S Commerce Department issues its advanced second-quarter gross domestic product estimate, which is likely to have increased 2.6 percent compared with a 1.4 percent rise in the previous quarter. The Commerce Department will also report that advanced core PCE prices for the second quarter are forecast to rise 0.8 percent, but lower than a 2.0 percent rise in the first quarter. (0830/1230) The final reading of University of Michigan Surveys of Consumers Sentiment Index for July is expected to remain unchanged at 93.1 from the previous month. (1000/1400) The Labor Department issues the second quarter Employment Cost Index, which is likely to have gained 0.6 percent. (0830/1230)

Investor focus will be on the performance of Merck & Co Inc's high-profile cancer drug Keytruda as the drugmaker reports second-quarter results amid rising competition in the lung cancer market. Investors will also be looking for comments on the multiple myeloma trials, which were testing Keytruda in combination with Celgene's standard of care treatments, and were placed on clinical hold by the U.S regulator earlier this month. Meanwhile, AbbVie Inc also reports second quarter results that are likely to be helped by increased sales of its flagship drug, Humira. Investors will also look for comment on its cancer drug Imbruvica, which analysts expect to become an important revenue driver for the drugmaker.

Exxon Mobil Corp, the world's largest publicly traded oil producer, is expected to post a second quarter profit. Separately, U.S. oil producer Chevron Corp is also expected to post a second quarter profit.

Baker Hughes reports second quarter results. The world's second-largest oilfield services provider, created by Baker Hughes' merger with GE's oil and gas equipment operations, is expected to report quarterly revenue of $2.34 billion and a loss of 15 cents per share in its maiden quarterly release. Investors will be keen on knowing how the company plans to run its business in an uncertain oil market.

Barclays Plc reports first half earnings, with alleged misdeeds by bank executives past and present threatening to overshadow the lender's financial performance. Chief Executive Jes Staley faces a regulatory probe into his attempts to unmask a whistleblower, while the bank has hit headlines in recent months over the trial of its former CEO and others for conduct during its crisis-era Qatar bailout. From a business point of view investors may focus on whether Barclays repeats its dire first quarter bond trading performance, a problem which U.S. rivals saw continue into the period ended June.

Credit Suisse Group AG reports second quarter results. After raising 4 billion Swiss francs earlier this year to plug a hole in its balance sheet, Tidjane Thiam will give an update on his restructure of Switzerland's second-biggest bank two years into his tenure as CEO. Investors and analysts are keen to see healthy inflows at its core wealth management businesses, an improvement at its global markets trading division - the source of billions of dollars in losses last year - and progress in winding down its "bad bank".

Goodyear Tire & Rubber Co reports second quarter results. The U.S. tire maker is expected to report a drop in profit and revenue due to a decrease in its tire shipments. The company has been struggling with a decline in heavy-duty truck production in the United States as a result of oversupply in the market. The company has also been cutting costs and has hiked tire prices to counter higher raw material costs. Investors will look for updates on its long-term forecasts.

American Airlines Group Inc is expected to report strong second quarter financial results. The No. 1 U.S. airline in its June traffic report raised guidance on closely watched metrics including pre-tax margins and total revenue per available seat mile.

The Federal Reserve Bank of Minneapolis President Neel Kashkari participates in a moderated question-and-answer session before a Woodbury Area/St. Paul Chamber of Commerce event, Oakdale, Minneapolis. (1320/1720)

Canada's Bombardier Inc will report second quarter earnings amid industry speculation that the plane and train maker is poised to form new rail joint ventures with Germany's Siemens AG. Bombardier executives, however, are not expected to discuss recent media reports that the two companies could form separate joint ventures in signaling and rolling stock as early as August. Analysts will be watching for an update on the company's cash flow and whether Bombardier's guidance for 30 to 35 CSeries jet deliveries remains on track for 2017. Statistics Canada may report that the Canadian economy grew by 0.2 percent in May. The report is likely to support analysts' expectations that the economy maintained its momentum in the second quarter after a strong start to the year. (0830/1230)

Brazil's IGP-M price index for July, which includes wholesale and consumer prices, is forecast to fall 0.65 percent. The index had fallen 0.67 percent in June. The country's inflation has plunged as the economy struggles to recover from its worst recession on record. (0700/1100) The unemployment rate is expected to remain unchanged at 13.3 percent in June from the previous month.(0800/1200) Meanwhile, the country is expected to post a budget deficit of 19.25 billion reais in June compared with a deficit of 30.70 billion reais in May.(1000/1400) Chile's manufacturing output is expected to fall 1.1 percent in June from a year earlier. (0900/1300)

LIVECHAT-WEEKAHEAD Reuters EMEA markets editor Mike Dolan discusses the upcoming week's main market inflection points. (0600/1000) To join the Global Markets Forum, click here http://bit.ly/1kTxdKD

(Compiled By Shradha Singh in Bengaluru; Editing by Shounak Dasgupta) ((Shradha.Singh@thomsonreuters.com))

and other income $‍62,876​ million versus $57,694 million.Quarterly ‍oil-equivalent production was 3.9 million oil-equivalent barrels per day, down 1 percent from prior year​.Quarterly ‍natural gas production was 9.9 billion cubic feet per day, up 158 million cubic feet per day​.Q2 2017 earnings of $3.4 billion increased 97 percent from Q2 of 2016.Q2 worldwide refinery throughput ‍4,345​ kbd versus 4,152 kbd.Q2 cash flow from operations and asset sales was ‍$7.1 billion versus $5.5 billion last year.Quarterly ‍chemical earnings of $985 million were $232 million lower than Q2 of 2016​.Q2 2017 capital and exploration expenditures were $3.9 billion, down 24 percent from Q2 of 2016.Quarterly ‍upstream earnings were $1.2 billion in Q2 of 2017, up $890 million from Q2 of 2016​.Quarterly ‍downstream earnings were $1.4 billion, up $560 million from Q2 of 2016​.Q2 revenue view $61.92 billion -- Thomson Reuters I/B/E/S.Says Q2 chemical earnings were down primarily due to higher turnaround activities, lower volumes, and decreased margins.Copyright (c) 2017 Thomson Reuters

EARNINGS-TICKER-Chevron macht wieder Gewinn - Reuters (German)

{{20170728T124053.734+0000}}EARNINGS-TICKER-Chevron macht wieder Gewinn28. Jul (Reuters) - Zahlreiche Firmen veröffentlichen dieser Tage ihre aktuelle Quartalsbilanz. Es folgt in Kurzform ein Überblick über einige Ergebnisse vom Freitag:

14.32 Uhr - Chevron hat im abgelaufenen Quartal wieder Gewinn gemacht. Hintergrund waren gesunkene Kosten und eine gestiegene Produktion. Der Nettogewinn des Ölkonzerns belief sich auf 1,45 Milliarden Dollar. Ein Jahr zuvor stand noch ein Verlust von 1,47 Milliarden Dollar in der Bilanz.

14.05 Uhr - Der Ölkonzern Exxon Mobil hat seinen Gewinn im abgelaufenen Quartal fast verdoppelt. Der Überschuss legte auf 3,35 Milliarden Dollar zu nach 1,7 Milliarden ein Jahr zuvor. Exxon förderte allerdings weniger Öl, die Produktion fiel ein Prozent.

13.38 Uhr - Steigende Ticketpreise und ein höheres Passagieraufkommen verhelfen American Airlines zu mehr Umsatz. Die Erlöse legten im abgelaufenen Quartal um 7,2 Prozent auf 11,11 Milliarden Dollar zu. Dennoch fiel der Nettogewinn auf 803 Millionen Dollar von zuvor 950 Millionen Dollar.

13.32 Uhr - Goodyear hat Mühe beim Verkauf seiner Reifen. Der Überschuss fiel im abgelaufenen Quartal um 27,2 Prozent auf 147 Millionen Dollar. Mit 3,69 Milliarden Dollar setzte der Konzern knapp fünf Prozent weniger um als vor einem Jahr.

12.51 Uhr - Der US-Pharmakonzern Merck & Co punktet mit seinem neuartigen Krebsmittel Keytruda. Dank der guten Verkäufe des Medikaments schoss der Nettogewinn im abgelaufenen Quartal um 61,5 Prozent auf 1,95 Milliarden Dollar nach oben. Der Umsatz stieg binnen Jahresfrist auf 9,93 von 9,84 Milliarden Dollar.

12.07 Uhr - Der Flugzeug- und Zugbauer Bombardier hat im abgelaufenen Quartal mit 4,1 Milliarden Dollar fünf Prozent weniger eingenommen als ein Jahr zuvor. Dennoch erzielte der kanadische Konzern einen bereinigten Nettogewinn von 39 Millionen Dollar. Im Vorjahreszeitraum war noch ein Verlust von 83 Millionen Dollar angefallen.

09.25 Uhr - Der Waschanlagenbauer Washtec hat im ersten Halbjahr den Umsatz um fast ein Viertel auf knapp 210 Millionen Euro gesteigert, während der Gewinn vor Steuern um mehr als 60 Prozent auf 25 Millionen Euro sprang. Im Gesamtjahr will das Unternehmen nun mindestens einen Umsatz von 420 Millionen Euro und eine Gewinnmarge von zwölf Prozent schaffen.

09.10 Uhr - Der Triebwerksbauer MTU Aero hat im zweiten Quartal bei Umsatz und Ergebnis die Erwartungen des Finanzmarktes übertroffen. Das Unternehmen erwirtschaftete einen operativen Gewinn von 164 (Prognose: 148) Millionen Euro und einen Umsatz von 1,286 (1,27) Milliarden Euro. Für das Gesamtjahr peilt es nun Erlöse von 5,3 statt 5,1 bis 5,2 Milliarden Euro an.

09.00 Uhr - Der französische Autokonzern Renault hat im ersten Halbjahr bei Absatz und Gewinn neue Rekorde eingefahren. Der operative Gewinn stieg um fast ein Fünftel auf 1,82 Milliarden Euro. Netto standen 2,4 Milliarden Euro zu Buche - nicht zuletzt dank eines hohen Gewinnbeitrags der Beteiligung Nissan<7201.T>, deren Ergebnis sich um mehr als 70 Prozent verbesserte.

08.27 Uhr - Der britische Telekomkonzern BT hat im abgelaufenen Quartal einen 42-prozentigen Einbruch des Vorsteuergewinns auf 418 Millionen Pfund (rund 468 Millionen Euro) hinnehmen müssen. Sonderlasten nach einem Bilanzskandal in Italien und einer Einigung mit der Deutschen Telekom und der französischen Orange waren dafür verantwortlich.

08.20 Uhr - Der Verkauf von Geschäftsteilen in Afrika kommt die britische Großbank Barclays teuer zu stehen. Durch die Trennung entstand in der Bilanz des ersten Halbjahres ein Verlust von 1,2 Milliarden Pfund, wie das Institut am Freitag mitteilte. Ohne diesen Sondereffekt lag der Halbjahresgewinn vor Steuern bei 2,3 Milliarden Pfund und damit 300 Millionen Pfund höher als im ersten Halbjahr 2016. Analysten hatten von den Briten allerdings einen Vorsteuergewinn von 2,7 Milliarden Pfund erwartet.

08.10 Uhr - Der französische Versorger Engie hat seinen Umsatz in der ersten Jahreshälfte leicht auf 33,1 Milliarden Euro gesteigert. Der Gewinn stagnierte bei fünf Milliarden Euro. Der Konzern bestätigte seine Jahresziele und sieht sich beim Umbau, der im kommenden Jahr abgeschlossen werden soll, über Plan.

08.00 Uhr - Die in Paris ansässige Mehrländer-Börse Euronext hat trotz der mauen Aktivität vieler Anleger im zweiten Quartal ihren Gewinn gesteigert. Das operative Ergebnis sei auf 79,2 (206: 77,7) Millionen Euro gestiegen, teilte der Betreiber von Kassa- und Derivate-Börsen in Paris, Amsterdam, Brüssel, London und Lissabon mit. Während andere Börsenbetreiber wie die Deutsche Börse teilweise von schwächeren Umsätzen berichtet hatten, stieg der tägliche Derivatehandel auf Euronext-Plattformen im zweiten Quartal um 27,3 Prozent.

07.50 Uhr - Die Fluggesellschaft Air France-KLM hat im zweiten Quartal von einem anziehenden Reisegeschäft profitiert und ihren Umsatz um 1,5 Prozent steigern können. Der operative Gewinn lag mit 496 Millionen Euro leicht über den Erwartungen von Branchenanalysten. Der französisch-niederländische Konzern veröffentlichte keine Jahresprognose, Analysten erwarten jedoch einen Jahresgewinn von rund 1,3 Milliarden Euro.

07.45 Uhr - Der französische Energieriese Electricite de France hat im ersten Halbjahr einen deutlichen Gewinnrückgang verkraften müssen. Das operative Ergebnis sei um ein Fünftel auf sieben Milliarden Euro abgerutscht, teilte das Unternehmen mit und machte dafür "unvorteilhafte Marktbedingungen" verantwortlich. Unter dem Strich blieb ein Gewinn von zwei Milliarden Euro - ein Minus von 3,7 Prozent. Seine Jahresziele bestätigte der Konzern.

07.40 Uhr - Der IT-Vermieter Grenke hat seinen Gewinn im ersten Halbjahr um fast 20 Prozent auf 78,8 Millionen Euro gesteigert und erhöht deshalb seine Prognose für das Gesamtjahr leicht. Es werde nun ein Jahresgewinn zwischen 118 und 124 Millionen Euro erwartet. Bislang war das Unternehmen von 113 bis 123 Millionen Euro ausgegangen.

07.32 Uhr - Der französische Gasekonzern Air Liquide hat im ersten Halbjahr Umsatz und Gewinn kräftig gesteigert. Unter dem Strich erwirtschaftete der Konkurrent des deutschen Linde-Konzerns in den ersten sechs Monaten 928 Millionen Euro, ein Plus von 14,5 Prozent. Der operstive Gewinn sprang sogar um mehr als 20 Prozent nach oben.

07.25 Uhr - Die spanische Großbank Santander hat dank eines brummenden Geschäfts in ihrem größten Markt Brasilien den Gewinn im zweiten Quartal um fast 40 Prozent auf 1,75 Milliarden Euro gesteigert. Das Institut hatte Anfang Juni den angeschlagenen heimischen Konkurrenten Banco Popular übernommen.

07.20 Uhr - Der erwartete Gewinnrückgang bei der französischen Großbank BNP Paribas fiel im zweiten Quartal dank Kostensenkungen und eines überraschend guten Geschäfts im Investmentbanking niedriger aus als erwartet. Der Nettogewinn von Frankreichs größtem börsennotierten Kreditinstitut sank zwischen April und Ende Juni um 6,4 Prozent auf knapp 2,4 Milliarden Euro. Von Reuters befragte Analysten hatten mit einem Gewinnrückgang auf 1,9 Milliarden Euro gerechnet.

07.10 Uhr - Der Spezialsoftwareanbieter Nemetschek hat im ersten Halbjahr seinen Umsatz um ein Fünftel auf 194 Millionen Euro gesteigert. Der operative Gewinn erreichte 51,7 Millionen Euro, was einer Rendite von 26,6 Prozent entspricht. Das Unternehmen beließ seinen Ausblick für das Gesamtjahr 2017 unverändert.

(Zusammengestellt in den Redaktionen Berlin und Frankfurt. Bei Rückfragen wenden Sie sich bitte an die Redaktionsleitung unter den Telefonnummern +49 69 7565 1232 oder +49 30 2888 5168.)Copyright (c) 2017 Thomson Reuters

UPDATE 1-Exxon profit nearly doubles, but falls short of expectations - Reuters News

{{20170728T122937.641+0000}}UPDATE 1-Exxon profit nearly doubles, but falls short of expectations(Adds earnings comparison, stock, details)

By Ernest Scheyder

July 28 (Reuters) - Exxon Mobil Corp , the world's largest publicly traded oil producer, said on Friday its quarterly profit nearly doubled on surging margins at its operations outside the United States, but results fell shy of Wall Street's expectations.

Shares of Irving, Texas-based Exxon fell about 1.9 percent in premarket trading to $79.30.

While Exxon's U.S. portfolio, including its shale projects, lost money, Exxon's gas and oil operations across the world posted a 69 percent jump in profit.

The company sold more gasoline and kerosene in the quarter, boosting the bottom line as well, but sales of chemicals slipped due in part to plant maintenance costs and weak margins.

"Our job is to grow long-term value by investing in our integrated portfolio of opportunities that succeed regardless of market conditions," Chief Executive Darren Woods said in a statement.

The company posted second-quarter net income of $3.35 billion, or 78 cents per share, compared to $1.7 billion, or 41 cents per share, a year earlier. Analysts expected earnings of 84 cents per share, according to Thomson Reuters I/B/E/S.

Production fell about 1.0 percent to 3.9 million barrels of oil equivalent per day.

The results come as Exxon battles its shareholders and others over climate change issues.

Exxon has been locked in an aggressive back-and-forth skirmish over climate change documents with New York State Attorney General Eric Schneiderman, who has sought to punish the oil producer for what he says are misleading public disclosures.[nL1N1IZ0N6]

Exxon's shareholders in May approved a resolution in May that called for the company to issue a report on how climate change affects operations. The vote, which was non-binding, passed with 62 percent of ballots cast and was a rare defeat for Exxon's management.[nL1N1IX15V]

(Reporting by Ernest Scheyder; Editing by Bernadette Baum) ((ernest.scheyder@thomsonreuters.com; Twitter: @ErnestScheyder; +1-713-210-8512; Reuters Messaging: ernest.scheyder.thomsonreuters.com@reuters.net))

Exxon Mobil casi duplica su ganancia trimestral - Reuters (Spanish)

{{20170728T122129.221+0000}}Exxon Mobil casi duplica su ganancia trimestral28 jul (Reuters) - Exxon Mobil Corp , el mayor productor de petróleo del mundo que cotiza en bolsa, dijo el viernes que sus ganancias trimestrales casi se duplicaron por los crecientes márgenes de sus operaciones fuera de Estados Unidos.

La compañía registró una utilidad neta de 3.350 millones de dólares, o 78 centavos por acción, en comparación con los 1.700 millones de dólares, o 41 centavos por acción, del mismo periodo de un año antes.

Exxon Mobil-Doublement des profits au T2  - Reuters (French)

{{20170728T121555.216+0000}}Exxon Mobil-Doublement des profits au T2 28 juillet (Reuters) - Exxon Mobil , première capitalisation pétrolière mondiale, a fait état vendredi d'un quasi-doublement de son bénéfice trimestriel grâce à la nette amélioration des marges de ses activités en dehors des Etats-Unis.

Le bénéfice est ressorti à 3,35 milliards de dollars (2,86 milliards d'euros) au deuxième trimestre, soit 78 cents par action, contre 1,7 milliard de dollars (41 cents) un an auparavant.

La production a baissé de 1% à 3,9 millions de barils équivalent pétrole par jour.

L'action perdait 1,2% à 79,15 dollars en avant-Bourse.
